</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International Names Deepak Iyer as </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>EVP&nbsp;&amp; President, Asia Pacific, Middle East and Africa </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">25+ year veteran Iyer has successfully led growth of businesses in India, Southeast Asia and Africa
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Maurizio Brusadelli to leave company in June to pursue external leadership opportunity<I> </I>
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>CHICAGO &#150; May</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;2, 2023</B> &#150; Mondel&#275;z International (Nasdaq: MDLZ) today announced
that Deepak Iyer, 56, the company&#146;s President, India&nbsp;&amp; Southeast Asia, has been named Executive Vice President and President, Asia Pacific, Middle East and Africa (AMEA) effective June 5. In his new role, Iyer will be responsible for
leading the company&#146;s $6.8&nbsp;billion AMEA business across more than 70 countries, which includes iconic brands such as <I>Oreo</I> and <I>belVita</I> biscuits, <I>Cadbury</I> chocolate and <I>Kinh Do</I> cakes. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;With close to three decades of leadership experience and a strong track record of success driving the growth of brands in emerging
markets across Asia and Africa, Deepak is the ideal leader to continue our strong and sustained growth across the AMEA region,&#148; said Chairman and CEO Dirk Van de Put. &#147;Under his leadership these past six and a half years, India has
delivered strong, profitable growth and become a consistent exporter of talent and best practices across our global network. We look forward to leveraging his skills and experience in this expanded role to drive greater positive impact across the
broader region and the entire company.&#148;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Since 2016, Iyer has successfully led the company&#146;s India
business driving sustained double-digit revenue growth, significantly expanded profit margins, strong cash flow generation and the adoption of advanced technologies and use of consumer data. An engineer with and MBA and more than three decades of
management experience across Sales, Marketing and General Management, he has successfully managed businesses across India, Southeast Asia and Africa. Iyer has vast and versatile industry and operating model experiences including time at PepsiCo and
Wrigley India Pvt Ltd. Importantly, he has built a top team in CPG, widely recognized for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> marketing, sales, sustainability integration, talent and
engagement and supply chain capability. Iyer replaces Maurizio Brusadelli, who will leave the company in June to pursue another leadership opportunity. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;I am thankful to Maurizio, for his leadership during these past seven years in AMEA
and for his three decades of contributions at the company,&#148; said Van de Put. &#147;Maurizio is a passionate leader who has played a key role in building our AMEA business into a growth engine of the company. I appreciate the foundation he has
built to set Deepak and the team up for continued success and wish him the best in his future endeavor.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (Nasdaq: MDLZ) empowers people to snack right in over 150 countries around the world. With 2022 net revenues of
approximately $31&nbsp;billion, MDLZ is leading the future of snacking with iconic global and local brands such as <I>Oreo, Ritz, LU, Clif Bar</I> and <I>Tate&#146;s Bake Shop</I> biscuits and baked snacks, as well as <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk,
Milka</I> and <I>Toblerone</I> chocolate. Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, Nasdaq 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit <U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U> or follow the company on Twitter
at <U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P>
</DIV></Center>
